[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Which is invoked by `avifImageYUVToRGB` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1844[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy for Dynamic Stack Buffer Overflow in avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is a **dynamic-stack-buffer-overflow** occurring at line [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/libavif/src/[0m[95mreformat.c[0m[39m` within the `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` function. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue stems from **inadequate bounds checking** when accessing Variable Length [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mArrays [0m[1;39m([0m[39mVLAs[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m used for the chroma spill upsampling algorithm.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Specific Issues Identified:**[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Incomplete bounds checking [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m774[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m782[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Only validates upper bounds [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`>=[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwidth/height`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m but ignores lower bounds when offsets are negative [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Missing bounds checking [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m798[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m818[0m[39m - THE CRASH SITE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: The dampening [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msection computes offsets `a` and `b` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich can be [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m or +[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and directly uses them[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min array accesses like `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` without any validation.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Array allocation pattern**: VLAs `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mimage->width[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mimage->height[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhave valid indices `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m..width-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m..height-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, but the code attempts to access [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindices that can be [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39munderflow[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or width/height [0m[1;39m([0m[39moverflow[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Detailed Fix Implementation[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix must add comprehensive bounds checking to **TWO critical locations** in the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspill upsampling code:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### **Fix Location [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Lines [0m[1;36m774[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m793[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mFirst spill distribution section[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace the incomplete bounds checking:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m CURRENT CODE [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m774[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m782[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint adjCol = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi%[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint adjRow = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj%[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m check the bounds[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi + adjCol >= image->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    adjCol = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj + adjRow >= image->height[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    adjRow = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith proper bounds checking that handles both lower and upper bounds:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m FIXED CODE:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint adjCol = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint adjRow = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Only compute non-zero offsets if we're not at boundaries[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && i < image->width - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    adjCol = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && j < image->height - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    adjRow = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj % [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Initialize offsets to [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39msafe default[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only assign ±[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m values when the pixel is NOT at a boundary [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e., when `i > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m AND [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mi < width-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This ensures `i + adjCol` is always in range [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, width-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Same logic for `j` and `adjRow`[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### **Fix Location [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Lines [0m[1;36m798[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m818[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDampening section - THE CRASH SITE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd bounds checking that is completely missing:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m CURRENT CODE [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m799[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m809[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint a, b;[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    a = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m[39melse[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    a = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    b = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m[39melse[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    b = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace with safe bounds-checked version:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m FIXED CODE:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint a = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint b = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Only compute non-zero offsets if we're not at boundaries[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && i < image->width - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    a = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && j < image->height - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    b = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Critical Note**: All subsequent array accesses at lines [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m817[0m[39m [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain unchanged because the bounds checking in the offset calculation makes them [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafe.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Why This Fix is Optimal[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### **Preserves Algorithm Semantics**[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The spill upsampling algorithm distributes chroma [0m[32m"spill"[0m[39m to neighboring pixels[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- At boundary pixels, there are no neighbors in certain directions[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Setting offset to [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m means the spill remains in the current pixel [0m[1;39m([0m[39msemantically [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect for edges[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Interior pixels continue to behave exactly as before [0m[1;39m([0m[39mneighbors receive spill as [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### **Follows Existing Codebase Patterns**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix follows the **exact same pattern** used in the bilinear upsampling code [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m912[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m938[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m within the same file:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m From existing bilinear code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m912[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m923[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mi == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mi == [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->width - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    uAdjCol = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    vAdjCol = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        uAdjCol = yuvChannelBytes;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        uAdjCol = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m * yuvChannelBytes;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis demonstrates that boundary handling by zeroing offsets is **already [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mestablished** in this codebase for similar neighbor access patterns.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### **Minimal Code Changes**[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only modifies the offset calculation logic[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to the array allocation strategy[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to the actual array access statements[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Preserves all existing functionality including multithreading behavior[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### **No Performance Impact**[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The bounds checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`i > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && i < width - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are simple integer comparisons[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- These checks occur once per pixel in an already slow-path function[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overhead is negligible compared to the floating-point color space conversion [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Verification of Fix Correctness[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### **Bounds Safety Proof**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter the fix:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**For horizontal access [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`i+a` or `i+adjCol`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If `i == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`: offset is [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, so access is `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` ✅ SAFE[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If `i == width-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`: offset is [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, so access is `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mwidth-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` ✅ SAFE[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If `[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m < i < width-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`: offset can be ±[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, giving range `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, i+[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` = `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwidth-[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` at extreme cases ✅ SAFE[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**For vertical access [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`j+b` or `j+adjRow`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Same logic applies with height bounds ✅ SAFE[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**For diagonal access [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`i+a` and `j+b` simultaneously[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Both offsets are independently bounds-checked ✅ SAFE[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### **Algorithm Correctness**[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe spill algorithm has two phases:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Distribution phase** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m774[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m793[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Distributes spill to neighbors[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Dampening phase** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m798[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m818[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Reduces excessive spill[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAt boundaries:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Distribution**: Spill that would go to non-existent neighbors stays in current [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpixel [0m[1;39m([0m[33moffset[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Dampening**: Reduction applies to current pixel only [0m[1;39m([0m[33moffset[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is the correct behavior: edge pixels can't distribute spill outside the image [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds, so the spill accumulates locally, which is exactly what should happen.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Testing Considerations[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix will resolve the AddressSanitizer error without breaking existing [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fuzzer test will pass**: The specific crash at line [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m is eliminated[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Existing tests remain valid**: No changes to test expectations needed[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Edge case coverage**: The fix specifically handles edge pixels [0m[1;39m([0m[39mboundaries[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat were causing the crash[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No regression risk**: Interior pixels continue to use the same algorithm logic[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Alternative Approaches Considered and Rejected[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### **Approach [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Use AVIF_CLAMP macro**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint safeIndex = [0m[1;35mAVIF_CLAMP[0m[1;39m([0m[39mi + a, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, image->width - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rejected because**: This would silently clamp indices, potentially causing [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmultiple pixels to write to the same location, altering the algorithm's behavior.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### **Approach [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Skip boundary pixels entirely**[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m || i >= width - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m || j == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m || j >= height - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rejected because**: This would leave boundary pixels unprocessed, creating visual[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39martifacts at image edges.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### **Approach [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Allocate larger arrays with padding**[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfloat uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mimage->width + [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mimage->height + [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rejected because**: This increases memory usage unnecessarily and requires [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffsetting all array accesses, creating complexity and potential for new bugs.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApply the following changes to `[0m[35m/src/libavif/src/[0m[95mreformat.c[0m[39m`:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m774[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m782[0m[39m**: Replace bounds checking logic[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change lines to initialize `adjCol = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` and `adjRow = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace conditional assignments with bounds-aware logic[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m799[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m809[0m[39m**: Add bounds checking for dampening section[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change lines to initialize `a = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` and `b = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace conditional assignments with bounds-aware logic[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No other changes required**: Lines [0m[1;36m810[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m818[0m[39m remain unchanged as they become [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafe with the fixed offset calculations[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m. Summary[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix strategy addresses the **root cause** of the dynamic-stack-buffer-overflow[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby adding proper bounds checking to offset calculations used in array indexing. It [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollows established patterns in the codebase, preserves algorithm semantics for [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minterior pixels, handles edge cases correctly, and requires minimal code changes [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith zero performance impact. The fix will eliminate the AddressSanitizer error [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile maintaining full compatibility with existing functionality.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
